<div id="review_1418903322" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1418903322" />
    <a title="Nessia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48014530-nessia"><img alt="Nessia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1445901629p2/48014530.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1418903322?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nessia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nessia" href="/user/show/48014530-nessia">Nessia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780007182817" href="/book/show/8471075-the-book-of-tomorrow">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1418903322&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1418903322" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17909542013779956291">"The Book of Tomorrow" is about a girl of sixteen years by the name of Tamara Goodwin. Tamara was brought up in a wealthy home and she was always spoiled. Thus, she is very disrespectful and has horrible manners. She lacks humility and she believes that she deserves everything. <br/><br/>Thereafter, she is stricken with surprise by the demise of her father. As a result of his debts, her father consumed medicine and alcohol simultaneously, which led to his death. Unfortunately, their home and properties ar</span>
  <span id="freeText17909542013779956291" style="display:none">"The Book of Tomorrow" is about a girl of sixteen years by the name of Tamara Goodwin. Tamara was brought up in a wealthy home and she was always spoiled. Thus, she is very disrespectful and has horrible manners. She lacks humility and she believes that she deserves everything. <br /><br />Thereafter, she is stricken with surprise by the demise of her father. As a result of his debts, her father consumed medicine and alcohol simultaneously, which led to his death. Unfortunately, their home and properties are seized and Tamara and her mother (Jennifer) must reside in a small town (in contrast to their city life), by Tamara's maternal uncle and aunt. Her aunt and Uncle; Rosaleen and Aurthur are very peculiar. She's constantly bored and looking for action. She soon discovers ruins that beckon her curiosity. She even feels that she is followed. Tamara reveals a ruined castle that she connects to. She befriends a nun that lives in town. Sister Ignatius makes Tamara feel comfortable and jubilant. <br /><br />From the inception of their arrival in town, her mother behaves quite strange. She remains enclosed and secluded in her room and seems to be depressed. Rosaleen tells Tamara that her mother is depressed due to the passing of Tamara's father. Rosaleen doesn't allow them any privacy or time together and is constantly cooking food. <br /><br />Thereafter, a traveling library arrives at their residence. The librarian and driver, Marcus, shows Tamara his books and Tamara (not an avid reader) comes upon an intriguing book with a padlock. The librarian doesn't have the key and, nevertheless, Tamara borrows the book. Sister Ignatius succeeds in opening the book. Tamara's life is changed by this book and she discovers her handwriting in the book. This book is a diary of a day ahead; "The Book of Tomorrow." She realizes that she rectify and change the future days ahead. She sees her mother's health worsening and decides to order a house-call by the local doctor. This doctor is the father of a friend of hers; Weasley. She reads the entry of tomorrow and discovers that Rosaleen will try to prevent the doctor's checkup. Tamara doesn't want to allow Rosaleen to intervene, and she knows that Rosaleen goes to the bungalow every day at a specific hour to feed her mother. Tamara decides to arrange the appointment at this hour. The doctor arrives and Rosaleen catches the doctor by surprise. Rosaleen doesn't allow the visit to occur by telling the doctor that Jennifer is merely depressed. Tamara is furious with Rosaleen and goes to Sister Ignatius for consolation. <br /><br />She discovers that the castle was ruined due to a fire and one child was burned within. Sister Ignatius says that the fate of this child is known to Rosaleen alone. Tamara decides to run away and they run away to Dublin (her home-town), where she and her companion (Marcus the librarian) break into her old house. They are caught by the police and Tamara is returned to Rosaleen and Arthur. Aurthur and Rosaleen come to pick up Tamara. Arthur has always been prevented privacy with Tamara and every time he wishes to speak with her, Rosaleen intervenes. Arthur sends Rosaleen to a shop and they are finally granted privacy. He attempts to reveal Jennifer's condition and Rosaleen turns up. They return home and Tamara opens "The Book of Tomorrow" revealing that tomorrow (her seventeenth birthday) a package awaits her in the wall of the bungalow. She also reads that Rosaleen will stand in the pantry in the morning. Tamara surprises Rosaleen and discovers that Rosaleen opens a pill and inserts the powder into Jennifer's porridge. Rosaleen doesn't notice Tamara's discovery. She retrieves her package and receives a gift with the words " Happy Birthday."<br /><br />Tamara calls in the doctor again and tells the doctor that her mother is being poisoned. Rosaleen takes Jennifer to the hospital. Tamara and Weasley her companion remain the home and Tamara decides to search for evidence of foul play. She finds an old photo album that show Rosaleen, Arthur, Jennifer,and a child; Laurie. They are all group photos. She now recalls a visit she made to the local cemetery and seeing this name; Lawrence (Laurie for short). Tamara and Weasley go the bungalow to search for evidence and discovers an abundance of pictures of her posted on the wall. The pictures are of her as a baby until the present. Rosaleen finds Tamara in the room and pushes her. She yells out and a man with abundant scars rescues Tamara. Weasley remained outside and upon hearing the noise comes to her rescue thinking that this man had assaulted her and locks him in the room. (Tamara rescues him later) She discovers that Lawrence and Arthur are brothers and Lawrence was the man of scars. Tamara discovers that Lawrence is her father. <br />Many years ago, Rosaleen's mother had worked in the castle and Aurthur and Lawrence lived there. Rosaleen was fond of Lawrence but received attention from Arthur instead. There was a ground-keeper in the castle with a daughter that Lawrence was find of. This girl was Jennifer. Many years passed and Lawrence remained with Jennifer and impregnated Jennifer. Rosaleen was jealous from the inception of their relationship. Tamara was born in the castle. Thereafter, two men arrived (George and Timothy Goodwin) to examine the grounds for an investment. George Goodwin was fond of Jennifer and Rosaleen noticed. Rosaleen informed Lawrence causing him to banish Jennifer from the castle. He requested from Rosaleen to deliver a letter to Jennifer. Rosaleen burned the letter and burned the castle. Jennifer understood that Lawrence must have died and she decided to marry George. Lawrence made a pact with Rosaleen that she would care for him. <br /><br />Tamara realizes that due to her new book she had discovered her true father's identity. She now lives with her parents happily ever after. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17909542013779956291" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I thought the story was going to be magical and have a slightly Christmassy feeling, however it was more a family drama. There was a small theme of magic but just not in the why I thought it would be. <br/><br/>It was a good book tho, just wasn't what I was looking for. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('68h9ukKtNpKyrX67qy6CDytVdN9Ne5pF61dNbitBBhqyRibUxUwZ20zrsFbJbW8x82zVvNJS0R4eza6279BPbA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

<span id="freeTextContainer17538269771975884286">Cecelia Ahern was born and grew up in Dublin. She is now published in nearly fifty countries, and has sold over twenty-five million copies of her novels worldwide.
